īḻattu ilakkiya vimarcaṉat tuṟaiyil tēciya ilakkiyak kōṭpāṭṭaip piracārap paṭuttuvatil muṉṉaṇiyil niṉṟa vimarcakarkaḷē 1950, 60 kaḷil ilakkiya vimarcaṉattil muṟpōkku vātattai, allatu mārksīya aṇukumuṟaiyaip pirayōkittaṉar. ka. kailācapati, kā. civattampi ākiya iruvarum itil mutaṉmaiyākak kuṟippiṭat takkavarkaḷ. a.na. kantacāmi, kē.kaṇēṣ iḷaṅkīraṉ, ē.jē. kaṉakarattiṉā,
pirēmji. cillaiyūr celvarācaṉ, ec.em.pi. mukaiyatīṉ mutaliyōrum ilakkiya vimarcaṉattil muṟpōkkuk kaṇṇōṭṭattaip
payaṉpaṭuttiṉar.

muṟpōkku vimarcakarkaḷ iyalpākavē ilakkiyattiṉ camutāya uḷḷaṭakkattil atika akkaṟai kāṭṭiṉar. ilakkiyattai oru kalai vaṭivamāka maṭṭumiṉṟi atai oru camūka cātaṉamākavum ivarkaḷ kaṇṭaṉar. oru paṭaippu veḷippaṭuttum toṉip poruḷait taṅkaḷ kaṇṇōṭṭattil matippiṭuvatu maṭṭumiṉṟi, ilakkiyattiṉ nōkkam, paṇi, payaṉpāṭu ākiyavaṟṟai varaiyaṟuttuk kūṟuvatu maṭṭumaṉṟi, paranta
arttattil ilakkiya vaṭivaṅkaḷiṉ tōṟṟam, vaḷarcci ākiyavaṟṟai iyakkum camutāyak kāraṇikaḷai
mārksīya aṭippaṭaiyil viḷakkuvatum ivarkaḷiṉ nōkkamāy iruntatu, 60-m āṇṭukaḷiṉ piṟpakutiyilēyē muṟpōkku vimarcaṉam itaic cātikkak kūṭiya mutircci peṟṟatu. itaṉāl 60kkup piṟaku ilakkiya āyvu, ilakkiyap pulamai, ilakkiya varalāṟṟuṇarvu ākiyaṉa īḻattil vaḷarcciyuṟṟaṉa. kalāniti ka. kailācapatiyiṉ tamiḻ nāval ilakkiyam, aṭiyum muṭiyum, oppiyal ilakkiyam, paṇṭait tamiḻar
vāḻvum vaḻipāṭum ākiya nūlkaḷum, kalāniti kā.civattampiyiṉ tamiḻc ciṟukataiyiṉ tōṟṟamum vaḷarcciyum,
nāvalum vāḻkkaiyum. īḻattil tamiḻ ilakkiyam ākiya nūlkaḷum mullaicāṉṟa kaṟpu, tiṇaikkōṭpāṭṭiṉ camutāya aṭippaṭai mutaliya avaratu kaṭṭuraikaḷum ivvakaiyil mukkiyamāṉa ākkaṅkaḷākum. ivaṟṟilē ilakkiya āyvukku camutāya varalāṟṟai ārāramākak koḷḷum pōkkiṉaiyum camutāya paṇpāṭṭu varalāṟṟu āyvukku ilakkiyattaic cāṉṟāka koḷḷum pōkkiṉaiyum camutāya paṇpāṭṭu varalāṟṟu āyvukku
ilakkiyattaic cāṉṟāka koḷḷum pōkkiṉaiyum nām avatāṉikkalām.

muṟpōkku vimarcakarkaḷ potuvākavē uḷḷaṭakka āyvukkē mutaṉmai koṭuttatāl, taṉippaṭṭa paṭaippukkaḷaiyum paṭaippāḷikaḷaiyum matippiṭuvatil cila tavaṟukaḷ nikaḻntuḷḷaṉa eṉpataiyum iṅku cuṭṭikkāṭṭa vēṇṭum. cilavēḷai veḷippaṭaiyāka araciyal kōcaṅkaḷaiyum karuttukkaḷaiyum veḷippaṭuttum paṭaippukkaḷum paṭaippāḷikaḷum vitanturaikkappaṭṭum, uyarnta cila kalaiñarkaḷ vimarcaṉattukku
uḷḷākkappaṭāmal otukkappaṭṭum uḷḷaṉar. ikkuṟaipāṭu 70 kaḷil muṟpōkku
vimarcakarkaḷālēyē paravalāka uṇarappaṭṭatu.

uruva uḷḷaṭakkap piracciṉai ilakkiya vimarcaṉattil oru cikkalāṉa piracciṉaiyākavē iruntuvarukiṉṟatu. itu paṟṟik koḷkaiyaḷavil cariyāṉa karuttukkaḷ muṉvaikkap paṭiṉum, matippīṭṭiṉ akanilaittaṉmai kāraṇamāka ceyalmuṟaiyil tavaṟukaḷ ēṟpaṭa atiya vāyppuṇṭu. evvāṟeṉiṉum 70 kaḷil ilakkiyattil uruva uḷḷaṭakka iyaipiṉaiyum ilakkiyattiṉ kalaip peṟumāṉattaiyum aḻuttum vimarcaṉak
kuralkaḷ muṟpōkku vimarcaṉa ulakil olikkat toṭaṅkiṉa. em.ē. nuḵmāṉ, caṇmukam civaliṅkam,
ē.jē. kaṉakarattiṉā mutaliyōr ivvakaiyil kuṟippiṭat takkavarkaḷ. ē.jē. kaṉakarattiṉā māksīya aḻakiyal paṟṟiya cila kaṭṭuraikaḷai pāṭummīṉ, alai, mallikai mutaliya itaḻkaḷil eḻutiṉār. caṇmukam civaliṅkam, nuḵmāṉ ākiyōriṉ karuttukkaḷ kaviñaṉ itaḻkaḷilum ēṉaiya cañcikaiḷilum veḷivantaṉa. caṇmukam civaliṅkam itu paṟṟi eḻutukaiyil,

"......eṅkaḷuṭaiya ilakkiyam eṅkaḷ vāḻ nilaiyai eṅkaḷiṉ aṉupavam ākkittara vēṇṭum. eṅkaḷiṉ uṇmaiyāṉa vāḻnilai piratipalikkap paṭṭāl antap paṭaippu niccayamāka iyakka iyal rītiyāṉa camūka māṟṟattukku iṭṭuc celkiṟatu. inta uṇmaiyai muṟpōkku aṇiyaic cērntavarkaḷ eṉṟu karutappaṭum cila vimarcakarkaḷ purintu koṇṭatākat teriyavillai. avarkaḷ muṟpōkku ilakkiyam paṟṟiya cila
vāyppāṭṭu urukkaḷaic cepittuk koṇṭu ematu uḻaippāḷar varkkattiṉ kalaivaḷattai
vaṟaḷac ceytu viṭuvārkaḷō eṉṟa accam emmiṟ palarukku uṇṭu" eṉṟu kuṟippiṭṭār.

piracārap pāṅkāṉa karuttu nilaiyil iruntu aṉupava nilaikku muṟpōkku ilakkiyam koṇṭuvarappaṭa vēṇṭum eṉpatē ivarkaḷiṉ potuk kōṭpāṭāka amaintatu.

4

tēciya ilakkiyak koḷkai iṟukkamāṉa araciyal cārpai veḷikkāṭṭātatāl potuvāka ellōrālum atu ēṟṟuk koḷḷappaṭṭatu. āṉāl muṟpōkku ilakkiyak koḷkai tiṭṭavaṭṭamāṉa araciyal cārpai uḷḷaṭakkuvataṉāl ataṟku etirāṉa ilakkiyak kōṭpāṭukaḷ uruvākuvataṟku atu vaḻikōliyatu. anta vakaiyil 1960 kaḷiṉ piṟpakutiyil īḻattu vimarcaṉa ulakil iraṇṭu putiya ilakkiyak koḷkaikaḷ muṉvaikkap paṭṭaṉa.
oṉṟu naṟpōkku ilakkiyam, maṟṟatu pirapañca yatārtta vātam.

naṟpōkku ilakkiyak koḷkaiyai muṉvaittavar es. poṉṉutturaiyāvar. 1950 kaḷil muṟpōkku eḻuttāḷar caṅkattuṭaṉ iṇaintu niṉṟu 'makkaḷ ilakkiya'ttai ātarittup putumai ilakkiyam itaḻil kaṭṭurai eḻutiya es.po. 60 kaḷil muṟpōkku ilakkiyattiṉ piratāṉa etir vimarcakarkaḷuḷ oruvarāka māṟiṉār. muṟpōkku eṉṟa collukku etirāka naṟpōkku eṉpataip payaṉpaṭuttiyarait tavira tiṭṭamāṉa
karuttukkaḷ etaiyum avar muṉvaikkavillai. ākavē īḻattil ivarāl maṭṭumē muṉvaikkappaṭṭa oru ilakkiyak
kōcamāka atu maṟaintatu. ciṟanta paṭaippāḷiyāṉa es.po. cila nalla vimarcaṉak kaṭṭuraikaḷum eḻutiyavar. eṉiṉum ākkappūrvamāṉa vimarcaṉaṅkaḷai viṭak kaṇṭaṉaṅkaḷilēyē ivar atika caktiyaic celaviṭṭuḷḷar. pantanūl mūlamum uraiyum eṉṟa ivaratu nūl ivaratu vimarcaṉa āḷumai virayamākkappaṭṭataṟkuc ciṟanta utāraṇamākum.

mu. taḷaiyaciṅkam pirapañca yatārtta vātam eṉṟa koḷkaiyai muṉvaittār. muṟpōkku ilakkiyattukku etirāka kāttiramāṉa vimarcaṉak karuttukkaḷai muṉvaittavar ivarē. muṟpōkku ilakkiyattiṉ cittānta taḷamāṉa mārksīya tattuvattaiyē ivar vimarcaṉattukku uṭpaṭuttiṉār. intiyāvil mārksīyam eṉṟa collaik kēṭṭālē āttiramuṟṟu avastaippaṭum veṅkaṭ cāmi nātaṉ pōl aṉṟi, mu. taḷaiyaciṅkam
mārksīyattai oru tattuvārtta camayavaḻi niṉṟu vimarcittār. mārksīyattiṉ cila pakutikaḷai ēṟṟukkoṇṭu
ataṟku appāl cella vēṇṭum eṉpatē ivaratu karuttākum.

"mārksīyattai maṟukkum teḷivaṟṟa kalaiñarkaḷum cintaṉaiyāḷarkaḷum mutalil atai uṇarntu oppuk koṇṭāltāṉ avarkaḷiṉ maṟuppu veṟum maṟuppākavē niṉṟuviṭāmal iṉṟu carittiram kāṭṭiniṟkum putiya taruṇattai iṉam kaṇṭu payaṉpaṭutti mārksīyattaiyum mīṟi vaḷarum veṟṟiyāka māṟuvataṟku vaḻipiṟakkum. atāvatu anta uṇmaiyai oppuk koṇṭāltāṉ anta uṇmaiyiṉ aṭutta pakkattaiyum uṇaralām" eṉṟu
taḷaiyaciṅkam eḻutiyuḷḷār. mēlaittēya mārksīya etirppuc cintaṉaiyāḷarkaḷiṉ
karuttukkaḷaiyum aravintar pōṉṟavarkaḷ piratipalitta intiya āṉmika vātattaiyum oṉṟiṇaittatē ivaratu koḷkaiyākum. avar tamatu ilakkiyak kōṭpāṭu paṟṟi eḻutukaiyil 'iṉi varavēṇṭiya kōṭpāṭṭai 'pirañca yatārttam' eṉṟu kūṟalām; viññāṉamum āṉmika ñāṉamum, vāḻkkai ākiyavaṟṟuk kiṭaiyē pētam irukkātu. vāḻkkaiyē kalaiyākum. kalaiyai aḻikkum kalai ilakkiyattai aḻikkum ilakkiyam
ivaiyē iṉit tōṉṟap pōkiṉṟaṉa. atuvē meyyuḷ eṉpatu ivaratu kalai ilakkiyam paṟṟiya karuttukkaḷiṉ
cāramākum, antavakaiyil ivar tarkka muraṇ niṟainta āṉmikak kaṟpaṉāvātiyēyāvār. mu.poṉṉampalam, eṉ.kē. makāliṅkam, imaiyavaṉ mutaliyōr ivaratu karuttukkaḷiṉ celvākku uṭpaṭṭavarkaḷāvar, taḷaiyaciṅkattiṉ pōrppaṟai, meyyuḷ ākiyavai īḻattiṉ oru kuṟippiṭṭa ilakkiyac cintaṉaiyai veḷikkāṭṭum mika mukkiyamāṉa nūlkaḷākum. ivaratu ēḻāṇṭu ilakkiya vaḷarcci - avacarak kuṟippukkaḷ
eṉṟa kaṭṭurait toṭarum kuṟippiṭattakkatu.

ituvarai nām nōkkiyatil iruntu 1960 ām āṇṭukaḷil ilakkiya vimarcaṉak koḷkaikaḷ īḻattil cittānta rītiyil vaḷarcciyuṟṟaṉa eṉpataik kāṇalām. muṟpōkku ilakkiyam, tēciya ilakkiyam eṉṟa kōṭpāṭukaḷ kāttiramāka vaḷarcciyuṟṟatāl araciyal rītiyil atai etirttavarkaḷum cariyākavō, piḻaiyākavō tavirkka muṭiyāmal putiya kōṭpāṭukaḷaiyē muṉvaikka vēṇṭi iruntatu. ataṉ viḷaivē naṟpōkku
vātam, pirapañca yatārttam vātam eṉpaṉavākum.

5

ilakkiyattiṉ camutāya uḷḷaṭakkam paṟṟiya kōṭpāṭukaḷum aṇuku muṟaikaḷum iṅku vaḷarcciyaṭaintatu pōl ilakkiyattiṉ uruvam paṟṟiya vimarcaṉak kōṭpāṭukaḷum īḻattil ikkālap pakutiyil vaḷarcciyaṭaintaṉa. ilakkiya vaṭivaṅkaḷ, ilakkiyap pākupāṭu, ilakkiya racaṉai eṉpavai paṟṟiya cintaṉaikaḷai ivai uḷḷaṭakkiṉa. ivvakaiyil kavitaik kōṭpāṭukaḷai vakuttuk kūṟum murukaiyaṉiṉ oru cila
viti ceyvōm, murukaiyaṉum, kailācapatiyum eḻutiya kavitai nayam, ākiya nūlkaḷ kuṟippiṭat
takkaṉa. kailācapatiyiṉ ilakkiyamum tiṉāyvum eṉṉum nūlum ippirivil aṭaṅkakkūṭiyatē. puṉaikatai vaṭivam paṟṟiya civattampiyiṉ puṉaikataiyum kataippiṉṉalum eṉṉum kaṭṭuraiyum kavitai nāṭakam paṟṟi em.ē. nuḵmāṉ, mu. poṉṉampalam ākiyōr eḻutiya kaṭṭuraikaḷum, putuk kavitaiyiṉ amaippu paṟṟi ciṟipati, capā jeyarācā ākiyōr eḻutiya cila kaṭṭuraikaḷum ilakkiya vaṭivaṅkaḷ paṟṟiya
kuṟippiṭattakka kaṭṭuraikaḷākum

ilakkiya vimarcaṉam, ilakkiyak koḷkai, ilakkiya varalāṟu ākiyavai taṉittaṉit tuṟaikaḷ eṉiṉum avai muṟṟilum vēṟupaṭṭavai alla. oṉṟai oṉṟu cārntum uḷḷaṭakkiyum celvaṉa. avvakaiyil vimarcaṉa pūrvamāṉa ilakkiya varalāṟṟu nūlkaḷ cilavum iṅku tōṉṟiṉa. ivvakaiyil pērāciriyar vi. celvanāyakattiṉ tamiḻ ilakkiya varalāṟu palarukku ātarcamākavum muṉṉōṭiyākavum amaintatu. kalāniti
ā. vēluppiḷḷaiyiṉ tamiḻ ilakkiyattiṉ kālamum ilakkiyattiṉ īḻattaṟiñar peru muyaṟcikaḷ, kaṉaka
centinātaṉiṉ īḻattu ilakkiya vaḷarcci, cokkaṉiṉ īḻattu nāṭaka ilakkiya vaḷarcci, cuppiramaṇiya aiyariṉ īḻattut tamiḻ nāval ilakkiyam mutaliya nūlkaḷ ivvakaiyil kuṟippiṭattakkaṉa.

taṉippaṭṭa paṭaippukkaḷ paṭaippāḷikaḷ paṟṟi vimarcaṉa pūrvamāṉa matippīṭukaḷ iṅku perumaḷavu ceyyappaṭavillai eṉiṉum kuṟippiṭattakka cila muyaṟcikaḷ naṭaipeṟṟuḷḷaṉa. kailācapatiyiṉ iru makākavikaḷ, civattampiyiṉ tamiḻc ciṟukataiyiṉ tōṟṟamum vaḷarcciyum, tillainātaṉiṉ vaḷḷuvar mutal pāratitācaṉ varai, cempiyaṉ celvaṉiṉ īḻattut tamiḻ ciṟukatai maṇikaḷ ākiya nūlkaḷ ivvakaiyil
kuṟippiṭat takkaṉa. ivaṟṟuḷ cempiyaṉ celvaṉiṉ nūlē muṟṟilum īḻattup paṭaippāḷikaḷ paṟṟiyatu.
ivvakaiyil mahākavi paṟṟi caṇmukam civaliṅkam, em.ē. nuḵmāṉ ākiyōr eḻutiya kaṭṭuraikaḷum kuṟippiṭat takkaṉa. taṉippaṭaippu eṉṟa vakaiyil mahākaviyiṉ cātāraṇa maṉitaṉatu carittiram paṟṟi caṇmukam civaliṅkam eḻutiya virivāṉa vimarcaṉam īḻattu vimarcaṉa muyaṟcikaḷuḷ mika mukkiyamāṉa kavaṉattukkuriya oṉṟākum. ivaitavira īḻattil, ilakkiya vimarcaṉattuṟaiyil ā.
civanēcaccelvaṉ, kalā paramēsvaraṉ, cittiralēkā, maṉōṉmaṇi caṇmukatās, mu. nittiyāṉantaṉ,
ce. yōkarācā, turai maṉōkaraṉ, ka.caṇmukaliṅkam, es.em.jē. paistīṉ, kē.es. civakumāraṉ, em.ec.em. cams, ci. meḷaṉakuru mutaliyōrum kuṟippiṭattakka muyaṟcikaḷ ceytuḷḷaṉar.

camīpa kālamāka īḻattu ilakkiya vimarcaṉa muyaṟcikaḷil moḻiyil aṟiviṉ celvākkaiyum kāṇa muṭikiṉṟatu, ilakkiyam moḻiyiṉāl ākum oru kalai eṉṟa vakaiyil moḻiyil aṟivu ilakkiya vimarcaṉattil naṉku payaṉpaṭa muṭiyum. mēlait tēyaṅkaḷil ittuṟai naṉku vaḷarcciyaṭaintuḷḷatu. tamiḻakattil aṇmaiyil veḷivanta muttuccaṇmukaṉiṉ ilakkiyak kōṭpāṭu eṉṟa nūlil moḻiyil aṟivu naṉku
payaṉpaṭṭuḷḷataik kāṇalām. īḻattil kalāniti caṇmukatās, em.ē.nuḵmāṉ ākiyōr ittuṟaiyil ciṟu muyaṟcikaḷ
ceytuḷḷaṉar. caṇmukatāsiṉ ākka ilakkiyamum moḻiyiyalum, kaviñarum moḻiyum, em.ē. nuḵmāṉiṉ ākka ilakkiyamum naṭaiyiyalum, īḻattu nāvalkaḷiṉ moḻi mutaliya kaṭṭuraikaḷ ittuṟaiyil ārampa muyaṟcikaḷākak karutattakkaṉa.



piṉṉiṇaippu

īḻattu ilakkiya varalāṟṟukku utavum nūlkaḷum ciṟappitaḻkaḷum

1. nūlkaḷ

kantaiyā vi.cī. maṭṭakkaḷapput tamiḻakam, yāḻppāṇam, 1964
kumāracāmippulavar, tamiḻppulavar carittiram, yāḻppāṇam, 1916
catācivam ā., īḻattut tamiḻkkavitai kaḷañciyam, koḻumpu 1964
catācivampiḷḷai ārṇōlṭ, pāvalar carittira tīpakam, yāḻppāṇam, 1886

2. ciṟappitaḻkaḷ

iḷanteṉṟal, tamiḻccaṅkam, koḻumpu vaḷākam 1971-72
tamiḻ cākittiya viḻā malar, ilaṅkaik kalācārap pēravai veḷiyīṭu, kalmuṉai 1975.
tamiḻ ilakkiya viḻā malar, ilaṅkaik kalācārap pēravai, yāḻppāṇam, 1972
tiṉakaraṉ nāṭaka viḻā malar, koḻumpu, 1969.
nāvalar mānāṭṭu viḻā malar, āṟumuka nāvalar capai, yāḻppāṇam, 1969.
pāvalar turaiyappāpiḷḷai nūṟṟāṇṭu viḻā malar, nūṟṟāṇṭu viḻāccapai veḷiyīṭu, yāḻppāṇam,1972.
putumai ilakkiyam, tēciya orumaippāṭṭu eḻuttāḷar mānāṭṭu malar, ilaṅkai muṟpōkku eḻuttāḷar caṅkam, koḻumpu, 1975.
